de l’enfleure des piez	of the wrapping of the nails
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire; et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	When the nails are wrapped with what is hydrous, and are plain like citrine, it is necessary to cauterize on the back of the pierced finger between the auricle and the anus; and gently hold the cauterization with your hand without turning it.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too much on the front, otherwise it will be too tight, and let the awl of the citron be in, and follow the cauterization according to this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire; et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe; et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse; aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	Afterward, make two cauterizations on each leg at the pointed end of the cuticle; and let one be long and the other short, in front of the thigh and the other behind, according to the leg; and leave the cauterizations for a long time to cure, that the awl may enter; after the cure of the other cures that we have mentioned.
de la menoison	of the menstruation
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures; et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule; et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	When the abdomen comes from cold and moisture, as long as the digestive and nutritious virtues which are in the stomach and intestines are swollen and inflamed, and cannot be cured by usual means; and you see the patient very suffering and of strong yellow color, if make a good cauterization on the stomach according to what is spoken of before or on the stomach, at the cauterization circle; and four cauterizations are made around the bowel subtle, and two cauterizations are made on the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see the moisture abundant and the patient suffering, then perform the fire cautery on the pointed end, and on each side, and make small cauteries on the stomach belt, because the cure is beneficial when it has good help.
de la cure des emorroydes	of the cure of the hematomas
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres: III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois; et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile; et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	When the hematomas are either newly formed, or one or more, and they are old and have large amounts of cold, moist, corrupted humors, and are treated as we have said in divisions, and if not beneficial, if cauterization is made: III on the spine of the back, which is completely deflected and bent in many places, and the cauterization on the belly II doses; and if you think that the stomach is cooled and the meat is not cooked, and the face swells, then the face on the stomach cautery as it is said before, and the liver, and the gallbladder at all the cauterization clavicles; and leave the cauterization over long ten days.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After treating the wound as much as it is healthy.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the chalcidite which is called "thelul
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit; et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort; fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit; aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez; et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	When you use thelul, if the fire cautery appears as a raser, then put it all burned on the thelul coped; and leave as much of your hand as the cauterization comes to the vein's birth, without cutting; do this once or twice, and if you have more thelul, cauterize each one as we have said; after treating wounds as much as they are healthy; and if you use a large fire cautery on a catapult, it will give more help.
de plaie mal curee	Of a wound poorly treated
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot endure tightness or opening, which we will tell in his presence if he falls ill that cannot be cured by burning, then cauterization is necessary.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When there is no fistula, and it is awake and has a slimy and moist tissue, if you provide enough of this substance, and make sure to keep all the tissue as it is, then...
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing; et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	After the cauterization is washed and rasped, and it is pulled out of the fistula according to the quantity that enters, and is reapplied as soon as the wound is clean and uncorrupted, once or twice, depending on the amount of ointment; and the patient is warned about the nerve that is involved, and large wounds.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans; aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement; et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font; et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	1. If the fistula is in the course of the uterus and intestine, if these were caused by these lews, and only to make this happen in the throat, and think that it is not a human being; after curing the throat as much as it is healthy, and if the lew is removed, and the materials are long bones, then it is certain that the throat is completely healthy; and if the materials are not long bones, then it is certain that the throat is missing, and the bone in the font. And so one of these that we will say in his throat.
de la maladie des reins	2. of the disease of the kidneys
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit; et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	When pain in the head comes on suddenly, and with large ventritis, and no woman is at hand, then it is necessary that you cauterize it on both sides of the head at the clavicle that we have mentioned before; and if we cauterize it in a minute, there will be three caustics in line, and they will do more good.
de la vessie	of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce; et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing; et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	When the bladder is large and weak due to headache and moisture, if the patient retains urine, then it is necessary to cauterize in the part called the funnel above the bladder, either on the left or right, and so that each cauterizes once; and cauterize the back of the funnel, or II may do it twice; and so the cauterizations are clavicle according to the form mentioned before.
de la marris	Of the marriage
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde; et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor: adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos; et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	When the wife is cold and moist, and does not allow for conception, and the flow is corrupted and delayed; and when they come, they feel great pain: therefore it is necessary to make three cauterizations along the belly, as we have said or cauterization of the bladder, and it should be cauterized to harden the back. And if it is a cauterization of the clavicle, as we have said.
de la hainche	Of the hair
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble; et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle; et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	When the viscous moisture descends to the groove of the hair, and for this reason if it is silent from the limb, and the sign is that the thigh is longer than the other when measured together; and it is found that the legs are in different departments desired, if it comes that you cauterize the patient on the groove of the hair at the cauterization like a circle, and sign before the limb turning towards the groove so that the groove is in the circle; and if it is the cauterization such as those made on the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if this cauterization is not present, make three large olive-wood cauterizations, and they should be as similar to each other as possible; and the cure once it is healthy.
de la dolor de la hainche	the pain of the heel
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene: adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	When pain comes in the heel of the foot, and it is cold and moist, and the patient is cured as we have said in the division, but the disease is old: then it is necessary to purge the patient of large amounts of fetid pills or other bone-like pills.
Aprés li fai cautere; et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres: c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	After the cauterization; and the manner of cauterization is according to two methods: it is known as assembling hot medicines and cauterizing with fire.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz: que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire; aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	1. If the fire cautery is followed correctly, then some are like this: You should cauterize on the handle of the tail, using three triangular forms according to this shape, and making a good depth and large size between each cauterization of the spine, and it should be olive oil; never cauterize on the base of the tail, because there are four according to this form.
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche; mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	2. And if you see, if the cauterization is made at the circle we have mentioned in the dislocation of the tail; but make it in a way that the circles contain the entire tail, and all its points are equal, no matter how large or small they are.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	Here is the translation of the line: "And it is the way one does in sciatica, when the pain holds in the thigh, and does not reach the knee or the leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc; et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur; et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	Here is the translation of the line: "And if the pain reaches the knee and the leg, one should cauterize there, as the physician says that the pain holds, and one should cauterize the ankle four times, on the left side a small piece; and it is the cauterizing cutaneous, and the flesh that is most sensitive to touch; and if the patient feels that the pain spreads to two or three points or near the cautery which is called 'points', then it should be cauterized there.
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus; et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if the labor is difficult, I make him more; and if the pain is towards the thigh, I burn with the cauterizing iron or the circular one, and you do well to keep all your cauldrons that you do not burn too much the cauterizing iron but burn the nerves and the large arteries, and do not cause more harm and contraction to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	I have also seen others who made the cauterization on the ankle, and they burned so much that the leg became entirely blackened, and the foot, and it was noticed and corrupted all the feet.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a solution of the belly, where he died.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in two parts assembled, make a burn in one and the other according to this manner.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce; et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait; et c’est li forme:	And the surgeon said in the burn of the thigh, according to this manner, make it thus and so at the end as big as some large nail or less, and so by interlacing and so between them without spacing the quantity of a new piece; and they should be interlaced over two parts, and also like noses, and have a good handle; and this is the form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit; et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors; et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens; aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	1. And let it be washed as many times as it is all red and greasy, and then put on the handle of the malady's chisel, and make it bend on its own healthy cost. And the cauterization is once, and the cautery leaves three jors; and then apply ointment, and leave the wound open long enough; after the cure of the ointment as it becomes sound.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent; et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	1. Albucasim says that we use little of this cautery because of its pain, and we see little that uses it; and all this is like burns that can be endured, and either he afflicts or not.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi; et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	The first line of the text is: "Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi; et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche; aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After placing the handle of the axe on the patient's shoulder, gripping it firmly with both hands; after heating the handles of the axe in the warm water that is heated in the fire for one hour, and the patient suffers from the axe's chill and arsenic.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu; et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit; et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait; et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	For the burn is similar to fire; and when the burn has healed, use the instrument to lift the handle of the axe gently, raise it smoothly, and leave it for three days, and put on whatever is black in the bandage as long as the burn is black; and then leave it for three days until the skin is dry; and this will help after the cure of wounds as long as it is healthy.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument; et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	And if the pain spreads to the thigh or leg, make an instrument that traces according to what you did in the hair growth; and this is the way of the hot tool, and I have written or described the correction of medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Prepare alkaline and live charcoal, as much of one as the other, and mix them together, and put them in a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir; et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main; et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	Or if there is a small hole that the point of a razor cannot enter, and put in another pot well-plotted, and add alkaline and charcoal and soft ash, as much as you have two of the powders you will have well-mixed in your hand; and let it sit until it drips wax or can be poured, then take all of this wax and mix it with charcoal and alkaline as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	When the patient is cold and feels lightheaded from the medicine and cauterization of other parts, she will feel dizzy as if it were fire. And in other medicines where they burn the hamstring well, like hazelnut oil, anacardic acid, and chalcedony with soap, all these things mixed together will make her feel lightheaded.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	Galien tells us of a remedy where some were cured of the pain in the thigh and sciatica, and he was convinced that no other cure was needed, and that it would be completely cured in one session after this remedy was applied, and he was bathed as he instructed afterwards.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie; et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	And then in part, as you prescribe to take a piece of fresh and dry vervain, and make it with a little grease, and put on the shoulder, and on the thigh, and on the leg where the pain is, and leave it for three hours, and according to the quantity that the patient does not feel the tightness anymore.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then I let it enter a bath as much as the chest is raised, and I let it enter a lemon, and the pain will disappear entirely and it will be healthy again.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And advises that no one should use such cauterizing medicines, unless it is after the evacuation of the heart.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout; et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	And Diacorides says that if the sciatic nerve is cauterized with the horn of a goat and it helps, then it should be done in this manner.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take the linen and oil it well, and place it in the hole that is between the little finger and the other, which is called the fossil.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains; et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee; et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	After drying the goat horn and heating it until it is charred, and then putting it on the linen, and leaving it as long as there are stains; and repeat this several times, until you feel by touch that it has reached the skin, and that the pain is subsided. And this method of cauterization is called "cauterization with goat horn".
de la dolor dou dos	Of the pain in the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether by touch or percussion, or from too great evacuation, or from the appearance of expanded cold matter, none of these appearances is worth cauterization, but rather from that which comes from the infusion of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir; et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»; et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	It is necessary after the patient has been purged of fetid pills or other substances, that you apply them to the back where the pain remains, three lines of the thread are marked, and in each line V cauterizations or more according to the skill and quantity that the patient can bear; and it should be done according to the cautery called "points"; and if you see, make III cauterizations or IIII at the clavicle according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor; et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	This disease often affects many children, and the signs of the beginning are when they have narrowed eyes as they cry, and fear; and you see the spine of their back and the appearance that comes with the other spines.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and it is cured, if the cauterization is done on the cauterizer according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	If the cauterization penetrates every part of the spine evenly.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see, if the cauterization is done at the end of the spine with the cauterizer touching lines 2 or 3, and they are points close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After curing the joint as much as it is healthy according to what we have said, and warned that you will not perform a fire cautery on the bone that is in the spine of the nerve.
de la dolor des jointes	of the pain of the joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere: fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	When pain in the joints is due to moisture that has expanded to each corner of the body, and when pain comes from blisters, which are properly called "gout," and when it is of cold cause and medicines do not cure it, then it can be cured by cauterization in this way: make a cut around the joint of the pain, and let it be olive oil according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if you wish to pluck at the cheek that is red, then burn it with fire cautery at the entire cautery as claimed "point".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire; et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if the pain comes to the joints and other joints, and this happens many times, then burn it with fire cautery at three or four points on each part of the olive cautery; and if you have skill for more, but do not hold your hand too long as the pain may increase.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pain descends to the joints and to the back, then apply the cautery we have mentioned in this chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes; et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main; et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	If the pain remains in the hand, make incisions every two lines; and if there is no more pain, make incisions at each joint and on the hair of the hand; and if the pain comes from the elbows or shoulders, cauterize each part, and govern the patient's behavior with words and prescribe medicine.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you make the patient behave and purge the filth, they will be cured by God's grace.
de la routure dou syfac	of the rupture of the face
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor; et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre; aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors; puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	If the rupture comes in gashes, and the wounds descend as cuts and it is new, then when you see that you are curing it, do not let it mix with the old; and use things that relieve the stomach, if it descends from the stomach; after which make it lie on your back between your hands, and command that it lick its own hair as much as it can, and tie it to your two thumbs, and sign 'closed' at the end of the rupture on the bone, and in a way that is resembles the other half of a circle around the corner of the corse; then wash the cauterization with the form of it:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	As long as it is white and has a glisten.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu; et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier; et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains; puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os; et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere; que tu ne le brulasses; et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	Then clean the bull's balls on your leg; and the surgeon will stain his hand to make sure they don't come out; work well on the thighs with the fire cautery, and put a piece of cloth on each thigh, and another on the other side that touches the thighs; then place the cauterization sign on all your hand, and hold it correctly and as far as you can reach the bone, and if you don't reach it the first time, repeat it again until you touch the bone; and be careful not to let the bull's juice come out when you do the cauterization, not to burn it; and so that the fire cautery does not kill or cause other harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And you question whether, when you have not come to the bone in the cauterization, your efforts are worthless.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure; aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee; aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee; et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	It is necessary that the cauterization of children be gentle according to the size of the bone, and for adults even greater; after three days, cure the patient with fire as hot as possible until the burn is healed; after treating other injuries as long as they are healthy, and let him rest on his back for forty days while the wound is well soaked; and it is necessary that his bandages be loosened for a long time, so that the dressing does not stick when he gets up to relieve himself in the chamber.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors; et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire; et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	And after forty days, when he wishes to rise, he will find a well-made girdle, and every four days; and he should rest, so that he works quickly and does not have too much intoxication of drink and spices, and too high braiding; and when he teaches this lesson, it is completely healthy.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will say after the cure of trimming in his chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	of the rupture of the belly
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur; aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit; et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	When ruptures occur in other bellies and are known, and you see that they do not grow any more, he should re-cauterize according to the quantity, and it is the third angle according to this form; after the cure according to what we have said; and no of the ancients has said that it should be cauterized at a three-angle according to this form.
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	The first sentence to translate is: "But the sign of the joint is that it is wide and has a rough surface, and another is that it is painful.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	The first cauterizations are less painful and difficult.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	There is no pain in any part of the body.
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes from nowhere, either from cold or injury, and this pain lasts a long time, and the remedy of medicine does not help, then it is necessary to cauterize at the cauterization point called "points", and to set the cauterization according to the length of the limb, its thickness, its frailty, its verticality, its location of torsions and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien; se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If the first cauterization is painful, that's fine; if it's not, then continue with another cauterization on the same part of the body, because it is customary for the patient to die in the member that is affected, as long as the patient is still alive.
de meselerie	Of the surgeon's tools,
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The tools of the surgeon are never used once by cauterization, and at the same time, the disease that comes from the putrefaction of flesh and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief: I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous; et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel; et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir; et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	Can you see the cauterization, when the disease is at its beginning, and it is cured according to what we have said in the division, and neither does it displace nor tire, and you doubt that corruption will spoil all the patient, therefore I do the cauterization on the head: I cut off the head, and the other towards the front at the end of the thighs; and they seize the horns, and the tail behind the hamstring; and it lasts so much with your hand that the cauterization reaches the bone, and as much as the wounds issue forth so that the vapors of large humors may issue forth; and I cauterize on the nails according to what is in front.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse; et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules; et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains; et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler; et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	1. If the wound is scattered everywhere; it is evident, if you cauterize it with these cauters we have mentioned or chief, and the cauters in one place, and the cauters on the spine of the collarbone, and the cauters on the spine of the back, and the grip and the other parts, and the elbows and the ankles, and the tendons of the knees, and all the joints of the hands and feet, and the fissures of the hands; and you will find nerves that are located below the skin, which you should not burn, and no time has been made for a cauter on the bone of the elbow, and the other on the stomach bone, and the other on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite; et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	When you perform more cauteries, the patient benefits more and does not feel pain in the cauterization as much as healthy people do, because the heart is already corrupted to some extent.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	It should be large and small according to the members and joints, according to what you will find in different ways with iron.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After curing the shoulder with flour for days with honey and other remedies until it is healthy.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre; et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur; puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	When the member is completely healed by medicines and oils and plasters, and it is not yet healthy, then perform cauterizations on the member according to its size and thickness; and insert one cure into the deepest part; then cure the wounds as they become healthy.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure; et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	And never once has a cauterization been made on the hand, arm, and back, where the nerve is silent and the member is not affected; and none enters if they are not aware of the members and the courses of the moving nerves in the body.
de albaras	of barbs
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color; puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie; et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	When the disease known as "albaras" is awakened, and the art of medicine does not help, then cauterize with a cautery a small piece, according to the amount of the heat, until the blenching is ostee and the color is mute; then use flour and lentils with rose oil and plantain leaves, and senna and aloe, for each part; and mix them all together, and bind with a bandage, and apply to the limb as long as it is healthy.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The cure of syphilis by cauterization
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When syphilis appears at the beginning, and you see it stop, if it is cauterized with the cauterization tool that seems like a circle, all around the entire circumference of the sore.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre; et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois; et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	And they all say that it is necessary to cauterize the area around the sore; and this does not seem strange, because I doubt that it will become ulcerated and corrupted, and I have always wanted this to happen once; and the most accurate thing is that it should be cauterized around the entire circumference of the sore, using the cauterization tool called "circular," as we have said before.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	From the inflammation that cannot be measured
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens; et tu la vues haster de meurer: adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant; aprés le laisse ensi.	If anyone has a disease called "adulatia", and it delays in measuring either due to excessive production or because of the patient's old age (that is, too much) and lack of strength, or because of tightness; and you see it hurting to measure: therefore, use cauterization outside of the mouth with small cauterizing points as they are pricked; after that, leave it alone.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For it will hurt to measure.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it hurting at all the cauterization, if the cauterization is hot, then its form is like this:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand in the environment of these diseases called "adubelati" as long as the cauterization has perceived the kind, and such cauterization that the patient feels defuers in a certain way that the course of the diarrhea is aggressive.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the cure, when it is perfectly healthy.
li cure dou feu par fer	the cure by fire with iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another way of disease called "corrodens", and it is nothing but a mangy of the limbs, as it eats the limbs just like dry hair.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est; aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	If you see this disease in the leg that can suffer cauterization by fire, then sharpen the cauterizations clavile as small and great, according to where the disease is; after cauterizing all parts until all corruption is removed, and nothing remains of it, that everything that is corrupted is not osteit.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	Then it is left for three days, and it is put on the burned parts that suffer from blisters with oil as long as the burns are not healed and all the corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the treatment of burns caused by fire.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin; et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	And if you see after three days that no healthy burns are born, it is good; and if not, then resume the cauterization on the parts that are still corrupted.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu; mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division: pren la quant tu en as mestier.	And this disease has never been cured by medical care in the place of fire cauterization; but all fire cauterization is greater help, and I have already said that the treatment of medical care in the division: take the amount you have skill in.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	Of the porings that come to the peel
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Often there comes to the peel because of defenses against a disease called "closed" according to our understanding, and it is a great thing that causes pain in the limb.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the cauterization of this disease is done in two ways.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	It is to know that cauterization is by fire, and cauterization with hot water.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges; aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou; et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture; puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	Cauterization by fire is when you heat it like a hot iron, and it is made of a thin piece of iron the size of a pen, and it is heated until it can pierce all parts, and it has subtle margins; after you put it all around the nail, turn your hand completely around the nail as it comes to the end of the nail; and it leaves three days before it starts to seep sweat; then I make a poultice of well-cooked, soft mallows with hay, and leave the poultice on all night, and the nails will be loosened from their roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then, treat the joint with ointment as soon as it is healthy.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude; et est en teil maniere: pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues; et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine; et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre; puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	Then, if the joint becomes infected many times, and in the hands and fingers, it may be that you need a hot iron cautery; and it should be done in this manner: take a nail or a piece of iron, or a thorn, and put it on the nail and the hoof, so that you do not get warts; then put the nail on so that it touches everything around, then put a hot awl, and hold your hand firmly, and press your hand as you turn until the edge of the nail touches the root of the hoof, and you will find the hot iron way through the root; then suffer the pain of the hot iron for a little while, then remove it, and it will fall off all its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	I then make another cut, as long as you have cut through all these that are in the course, then I will treat the wounds that engorge blood.
li cure dou trembler	I will treat it so it does not tremble.
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee; et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire; si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	If the patient trembles due to cold, or fever, or other causes, then it is necessary that you make four cauterizations or four on the spine, one cauterization between each spine; and one cauterization at the stomach with olive oil cautery; if it continues to tremble, and it gets healthier from the cold disease.
des pustules puans	of pustules that have appeared.
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	No time is seen by defeats the body, such as baths or pustules, that come from large corrupted materials.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule: un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	If it is necessary to burn the first time when they appear, cut a subtle fire cautery of mart or if the point is seized by fire, or of the cautery of Aristotle's root, or of the lenticular cautery.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez; mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	And never are cauterizations made at the beginning when they appear in this manner, and they do not grow warts forward, but are disordered by the superfluity that comes, and they are healthy; but it is necessary that this be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	When the artery is tied off
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses; et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	Many times there are great dislocations of blood from the artery that is tied off at the wound which comes to the pardefuers, or at the incision of the abscess, or at the fire cautery of the member, and similar things; and it is a sad thing to have to open the vein.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus; puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge; puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	And if there is none, then whatever you have to put your finger in the wound of the vein, and hold it as tight as you can until your finger is numb and no longer hurts; then heat the olive oil cauteries more or less depending on the size of the wound and how red they are; then I, or however great or small according to the wound and the leu in case the artery is out of place, put the fire cautery on the vein where you hold your finger, and hold the cautery there until it is no longer burning.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	If the fire cautery is still burning when you tie your child's vein, and it has stopped, then quickly take another one that is hot.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez; et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide; et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit: ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc; et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	And continue to do this one after another until the wound is fully healed; and be careful not to burn the flesh that is sensitive, and avoid other harm coming to the patient; and know that as soon as you do not cut through the artery, it cannot well heal immediately once the artery is large, if it is not by one of the four methods we have mentioned: either by cauterization or extraction when it is properly treated, or by very gentle twisting, or by medicines placed on it that can cause inflammation; and make sure to tie and extract it carefully.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Whoever will tightly fasten the hair with strings or tourniquets, or other similar things, should not profit from it if it does not work.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne; et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez; et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	And if there is none and there is no remedy or medicine present, then he must put his index finger on the wound of the vein as we have said, and then firmly press until it is sore from the wound and the vein; and he should not move much, but his hand is often cold so that it does not freeze and becomes numb and sore; and he should make sure to use tools and medicines for cauterization.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	Here comes the first sentence to translate:
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres; et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	1. We have told you in the first chapter about all diseases, whether it is to cauterize with fire or with burning medicine, and their causes, effects, and forms of cauterizations; and I have put this chapter of cauterizations in the hands of the chief surgeon, and I will go to this chapter by my own way because it is lighter to travel with the one who knows the way.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	2. For in the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things; where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	I warn you that you are doing madness.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For many ways of people come in treatments.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice; et de ces doit on avoir paor. It is only necessary for you to allow those who come to you who have this way, but put more weight on your honor than in your counsel, and do not believe everything that seems certain to you, and that you can have taken or lost; and use divination and indication in the cures of your patients according to the health of the patient; and this will help you to this good reputation, glory, and memory.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Very good advice, my Lords, you will receive a good understanding and direction, and if you will seek the holy inspiration of his hand, amen.

dou chief plein d’aigue	dou chief plein d'aigue means "the head full of sweat
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant; et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	This disease often occurs in children many times in infancy, and when the child is pulled too hard on the head, and never has it been caused by anything else that is known.

de emigrainne	The first sentence to translate is "de emigrainne

de l’estoupement des oreilles	of the earache
Tout ceu que chiet ens oreilles est une des IIII choses: ou grains, ou beste, ou piere de mine ou semblans chose si com fer; ou semence, si com jaisses, feves, pois; ou chose defluans si com aigue et aisilz et semblans choses.	All that causes pain in the ears is one of four things: grains, bees, mines, or similar things like that; or seeds, like jaisses, feves, pois; or things that flow like fever and ague and similar things.
Quant il chiet en l’oreille piere ou autre maniere de chose que ne s’ajoste mie a l’oreille, ne ne croist en l’oreille, si met l’oreille au solel.	When the ear pains in the ear or in any other way than it does not fit well with the ear, and does not grow in the ear, put the ear to the sun.

If you see the wound, and it does not distill any drop of violet or thread oil, then perform extraction; I make the condiement, and it smokes the nostrils as it is extracted, and put the ear with pieces of linen or wool; and the ear remains in place.
Mout de fois vient fuer par ceste cure; et s’elle ne vient fuer, se li amenistre extraction as pinceures subtilz, de coi ci est li forme:	This remedy is used many times; and if it does not work, then perform extraction with fine tweezers, as follows:
S’elle saut fuer as pinceures, c’est boin; se ceu non, si amenistre extraction a l’oncine subtil de petite doubleure; et s’elle ne saut par ceu, si fai une caine d’arain et boute lou chief de la cainne ou pertuis de l’oreille fort, et estoupe ceu qui est entor la cainne de cire mole si que li vens n’i puisse entrer avec la cainne; puis le trai fuer forment, car mout de fois vient fuer si com nos avons dit; et s’elle ne vient fuer en teil maniere, si prent glut de coi en prent les oisiaus, et met en som aucun estrument qui soit a point por ceu faire, et met un poc de coton entor; puis presse le glut sus la piere ou quel chose que ce soit, et trai fuer.	If it jumps out with the tweezers, it is good; if not, then perform extraction with a small forceps and a double loop; and if it does not jump out, then make a gouge in the bone and bite off the end of the thread or ear hole, and smoke it that it does not enter through the candle wax when it comes, and then take form again, as we have said; and if it does not come out in this way, then take some lint and put it in the ear; then press the gouge with the tweezers or something else, and take form again.
Et s’elle ne saut fuer de toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si te haste de fendre l’oreille ainsois que aposteme chalz i veigne, et spasme; et li maniere de la fendure si est que tu faices premier sainier lou malaide de la cephalique, et estrai dou sanc selonc la mesure de sa vertu, puis fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains et li torne l’oreille au desus, et fent une petite fendure en la racine de l’oreille a la graisse ou leu dependant; et soit li fendure ausi com une lune, tant que tu viegnes a la piere, puis l’oste selonc ton pooir, et la suce hastanment a ta bouche; et la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	If she does not jump from all these things that we have said, if you continue to hit the ear even though it is swollen and spasms, and the manner of hitting if it is that you first clean the ear with the physician's scalpel according to its strength, then hold the ear between your hands and turn the ear towards the opposite side and make a small cut at the root of the ear in the grease or where it hangs; and let the cut be as full as you go to the hole, then the bone according to your power, and the saliva drips into your mouth; and the cure as soon as it is healthy.
Et se c’est grains qui est ens et il enfle, si aministre extraction; et si’il ne puet issir, si amenistre I spatumile tenve subtil selonc ceste forme:	And if it is gravel that is in and it flows, then apply the extraction; and if it cannot be excreted, then administer this solution subtly according to this form:
et amenistre incision de celui grain.	and make an incision on that gravel.
Mais ne faire mie ceu quant tu penses que li grains est moistes por la moistor de l’oreille, tant que tu en aies fait maintes pieces; puis l’estrai as pinceures subtilz et au succier, si com nos avons dit, si que li estractions soit aligie.	But do not force it if you think the gravel is moist from the moisture in the ear, as many pieces as you can; then extract it with gentle pliers and saliva, as we have said, if the extractions are successful.
En l’aigue donques que chiet en l’oreille covient que li malaides use d’esternuement de condisi premiers, et ample l’oreille de viel coton.	In the ear, therefore, if the gravel is in the ear, then the surgeon should use a soft excision and enlarge the ear with fluffy cotton.
Et soit gisans sus celle oreille meisme ou li aigue est.	And let there be caution with that same ear or the eye.
s’elle saut fuer per ceu, c’est boin.	If it jumps for this reason, it's good.
se ceu non, si prent maintes pieres selonc li longesce de ton doit tenves et legieres, et les eschaufe un poc au feu; et em mette li malaides une ou pertus de son oreille, et saille sus i. de ses piez d’autre part, et fiere d’une autre piere sus la piere qui est en l’oreille; et ne cesse de faire ceu de piere em piere tant que li aigue isse toute fuer, et ensi saut elle toute fuer; et se tu vues, si prent I jonc, et boute l’un des chiés en l’oreille, et l’autre chief emprent de feu tant que li plus dou jonc soit ars; puis refai autreteil d’autres jons tant que li aigue isse toute, si com nos avons dit en la piere.	And if it does not jump for this reason, then take many piercings according to the length of your wound and lightness, and burn them slightly with fire; and put the scalpel in your ear, and withdraw from there a little; and make another piercing on another part of your ear, and fierce on another piercing that is in the ear; and continue this until the wound is all out, and it jumps all out; and if you see, if it jumps, and catch one of the ends in the ear, and the other end take with fire as much as the more painful one is; then make another part of other piercings as much as the wound is all out, until the wound is all out, as we have said in the ear.
En l’estraction de la beste, s’elle est de petit cors, si com puce et semblans chose, cure la si com nos avons dit en la division; mais s’elle est de grant cors c’on la puisse sentir, si amenistre extraction de pinceures; et c’est li chose plus legiere a oster qui soit en l’oreille.	In the removal of the breast, if it is small in size, similar to a pea and resembles something else, it is treated in the same way as we have described in the division; but if it is large in size, one can feel it during the extraction of forceps; and this is the lighter thing to be operated on that is in the ear.
En l’estraction des vers enjanrez as oreilles, quant tu lou cures si com nos avons dit en la division et ou traitier des distillations, et li cure ne profite mie, si covient que tu regardes l’oreille au soleil: s’il i apert nulz vers, si les trai as pinceures subtilz, et s’il n’aperent, si prent la cainne de coi ci est li forme:	In the removal of the ears' tumors, if you treat it as we have described in the division and use distillations, but the cure does not benefit, then look at the ear with the sun: if there are no holes, if you use fine forceps, and if there are none, then take the rope of this form:
Et soit estroite desoz et large desus.	And let it be tight and wide around.
Et boute lou plus subtil chief en l’oreille selonc la quantiteit de la soffrance dou malaide, puis succe forment a tot la caine; fai ceu sovent tant que tuit li ver issent.	And pull on the ear more gently according to the amount of suffering of the patient, then gradually form a knot; do this often as often as it is needed.
Et s’il n’obeissent a issir, si estoupe entor la cainne de coton si com j’ai dit en la piere; et s’il ne saillent fuer si com nos avons dit, si aministre distillations que li ancien ont esprovees en l’ocision des vers, et tu les troveras ou traitier des distillations; et si distille tes oiles et tes medicines en l’oreille a tout cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme si com tu vois:	And if they do not come out, if the thread slips too far into the cotton glove as I have said in the incision; and if it does not enter deeply as we have said, apply distillations that the old ones have used in the decision of the verse, and you will find them or treat with oils and medicines in the ear at this instrument; and if you distill your oils and medicines in the ear as you see:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain estrois desoz a I petis pertuis, et desus overs por distiller; et por presser dedens la distillation a I estrument d’arain bien fait por ceu, et se tu vues pren I raseur et envoloupe entor la pointe avenanment coton; puis i giete ton oile ou ton jus, et ceu que tu vues de tes medicines en la cainne, et li caine soit en l’oreille; puis boute dedens lou raseur a tout lou coton, et presse ta main tempreement tant que li oile soit distilleit ou chevement de l’oreille; et lou sente li malaides dedens, et soit li distillations I poc eschaufee au feu ainsois c’on la distille en l’oreille; et garde qu’elle ne soit trop froide, car li medicine ne seroit mie si bone.	1. And let either silver or gold be boiled in the pierced holes, and then strained through a fine sieve; and to press the distillation into a well-made silver instrument, and see if you have a lancet and enfold it at the point of the needle; then let it drip your oil or juice, and what you see of your medicines in the vein, and the vein is in the ear; then dip the lancet into all the cotton, and press your hand firmly until the oil is distilled or runs from the ear; and it will feel the patient's pain, and so is the distillation in the ear; and keep it from being too cold, as the medicine will not be good if too cold.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	Of the ear's chill
Aucun enfant naissent qui n’ont nul pertus ens oreilles; et ceste meisme chose avient as homes par estoupement de plaie, ou de char nee dedens l’oreille, et cist estoupemens vient aucune fois em parfont en l’oreille, si c’on ne lou puet veoir; et aucune fois avient I poc defuer lou pertus, et lou voit om bien.	No child is born without having a cold in the ears; and this very thing happens due to a chill or from being exposed to cold air, and there is no cold ever felt in the ear unless it can be seen; and there has never been any sign of a cold, and it is well seen.
Celle donques que vient em parfont, si c’on ne la puet veoir, est de grief sanation em plusors dispositions, et en cele c’on voit covient que tu mettes l’oreille dou malaide au soleil; et regarde dedens: se tu vois l’opilation apparent, si la oevre a tot cest spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	That which comes on suddenly, if it cannot be seen, is a sign of serious illness in many cases, and in those cases it is necessary to put the ear with the cold in the sun; and look: if you see the formation of pustules, then the ear has completely this swelling of cotton wool, which is the form.
Et soit agus et trenchans devant et derrier tout plain, si qu’il ne blece l’oreille; se li opilation est de char nee ou cors de l’oreille, si la tien as pinceures subtilz, et la cope legierement, tant que celle chars soit toute ostee.	And so let the ear be cleaned and scratched all around, if it does not hurt the ear; if the dandruff is from the hair or the ear, if the fingers are gentle and the glove lightly, as long as the hair is completely removed.
Et se li opilations est em parfont en l’oreille, si pren I raseur subtil legier et l’eschaufe un petit au feu, puis li met ou cors de l’oreille.	And if the dandruff is fully removed from the ear, if I use a gentle and light razor and slightly warm it, then I put on a feather from the ear.
Se tu sens l’opilation dont li malaides sent grieteit a l’oïr, perce legierement, et garde que tu ne grever les ners de l’oreille; puis met en l’oreille une tente selonc la largesce dou pertus, et la moille en l’oignement egyptien.	If you feel the dandruff that the patient feels is gritty in the ear, gently remove it, and do not hurt the ear nerves; then put a tent according to the large pore of the ear, and apply Egyptian ointment.
Fai ceu aucun jor tant que li plaie soit soudee, ou tu pren une tente et la moille en aigue rose, et poudre sus vitriole broiet; et se tu vois enflee l’oreille, si couvient que tu traies la tente et remue une autre tente moillie en cerote qui soit fait d’oile roset et de cire, tant que li enfleure soit ostee; puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	For as long as the wound is not soothing, or you take a tent and moisten it with clear rose water, and powder it with vitrol broiled; and if you see the ear closing, then cover the tent and move another soft tent made of olive oil and wax that covers the wound until it closes. Then, when it is healthy, the cure can begin.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si plonge une esponge et drapelz en aigue froide, et le met sus l’oreille, et use d’autres cures qui oste lou decorrement de sanc qui sont ou traitier des destillations.	And if the blood flows out, then dip a sponge and wet it with cold water, and place it on the ear, and use other remedies that stop the flow of blood which are treated with distillations.
de la char des papieres	Of the parchment's folds
Cist althelul que vienent em papieres des eulz quant ils sont moiste et sont sec, si covient que tu les estendes de tenailles et de pinceures, et le cope d’un spatumile de ses racines; puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet.	That which is the thickest that comes from papers when the hairs are moist and dry, if it happens that you extend them with needles and tweezers, and the cope of a spatula of its roots; then put on the limb vitreous broth.
Et se sans en decort, si le cauterize dou cautere lenticulaire subtil, et li cauterizeir aprés l’incision vaut mues; et maintes fois repairent, cant aucune chose demoure de lor racines; et quant elles sont cauterizees par feu, si sont arses celles racines et ne revienent mie.	And if without decortication, if the cautery is a subtle cautery, and the cauterizer after incision is sufficient; and they are often repaired, no thing is worn out from their roots; and when they are cauterized by fire, if the roots are burned and do not return.
de la gresle	Of the grisely
Maintes fois vienent em papieres des eulz unes choses que semblent gresle en sa forme et en sa duresce, et por ceu est ceste maladie apelee «grandine», et est une assemblee de moistor grosse en la papiere desus et desoz; li ovraiges est telz: pren warde se li grandine se muet d’une part et d’autre, et c’est legiere chose a savoir; fent la donques dou large, puis l’escorche de chescune partie legierement, puis la prent as pinceures, et la cope.	Many times come in papers from the hairs things that seem gritty in their form and hardness, and for this is this disease called "grizzled" and it is an assembly of moisture large in the paper of it and out; the dislocations are such: take care if the grizzled is quiet on both sides, and it is light to know; then make it wide, then scrape each lightly, then take with pincers, and close.
se tu ne la pues coper sens percier un poc la papiere, si ne grieve rien au malaide; et se li fendure est grans, si l’assemble a une costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee; et s’elle est petite, si n’i faire point de force, car li oignemens la restoure tantost et enjanre char.	If you do not close it with care, it may tear the paper and cause pain to the patient; and if the assembly is large, it should be sewn at one seam, and cured as long as it is healthy; and if it is small, it should not be forced, because it may restore the rest too much and make it uneven.
Et se li grandine est dessendans au dedens de l’oreille vers la partie desus, si enverse la papiere, et estent la grandine a unes pinceures, et la cope et presse d’une part et d’autre; et se li papiere est esloignie par l’incision, ce ne grieve rien; et quant li grandine est copee, si leive l’oil d’aigue salee, et cure le leu de ceu qui enjanre char tant que li malaides soit sanez.	1. If the snowball descends towards the ear and reaches the inner part, and if you turn the paper upside down, and pinch the snowball with tweezers, and press the paper from both sides; and if you move the paper away with the incision, it causes no harm; and when the snowball is pinned, lift the oil of salty vinegar, and cure the lip that has turned as white as the malady so long as the patient is healthy.
de la graisse des eulz	2. of the fat of the hairs
Exinach est une graisse qui est enjanree en toiles des papieres desus, et ce avient plus as enfans c’a nules gens, et grieve mout a lor eulz, et li vienent li catharre as matinees, et ne pueent regardeir la lumiere dou soleil por ceu que les larmes se hastent a lor eulz; et por ceu se couchent il sor lor faices adés, et dorment sus, et sont lor papieres desoz lor sorcilz moistes que li enfleure et li apparance ont covert de l’exinach qui apert en l’oil.	3. Exinach is a grease that stains paper, and this happens more in children, and causes pain to their hairs, and they come to the cathouse in the mornings, and cannot look at the sun's light because their tears fall on their hairs; and for this they lie down with their faces turned away, and sleep, and their papers become soaked in their wetness that the exinach penetrates into the oil.
Et quant tu presses lou leu a tes dois et sent l’exirnach entr’ous.	And when you press on the joint with your hand and feel the excruciating pain within.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain; et puis pren I drapeil de lin, et appareille une tente em maniere d’un cercle selonc la quantiteit que conteigne exirnach de chescune partie, puis le met sus li; et presse a tes dois d’une part et d’autre, si que li exirnach soit assemblez emmi le cercle; puis fent em mileu de la moistor au spatumile trenchant une fendure dou large, et ne soit mie plus grans que li plaie c’on fait a la sainie de voinne; et fent le cuir em parfont tant que tu veignes a l’exirnach; et em plusors dispositions vient exirnach de la fendure, selonc la forme d’une piece de graisse blainche.	And the manner of the wound if it is that the patient places his head in your hand; then take a cloth from linen, and make a tent according to the quantity of pain each part contains, then place it over the wound; and press with your two hands on either side, so that the pain is assembled within the circle; then make a shelter of moisture at the incision, cutting a large, sharp edge, and not more than the size of the wound you made in the flesh; and make the cloth as large as you can see the pain; and in other ways, the pain comes from the cut, according to the shape of a greasy, white lump.
Estrai la donques a tout une piece de drap charpit entre tes dois au defuer, et torne ta main a destre et a senestre tant qu’il soit espars; et garde que tu n’ajoster en la fendure, que tu ne viegnes a tout le spatumile jusc’a l’oil, que tu ne le bleces.	1. Pull the thread through all a piece of cloth between your two hands, and turn your right and left hands as much as they spread; and make sure you do not pull in the fringes, that you do not go to any part of the suture, that you do not hurt it.
Et se li exirnach n’apert en l’encomencement de la fendure, si acroi un poc la fendure legierement tant qu’il apere; puis l’estrai si com nos avons dit, puis moille drapelz en aisil et en aigue, et met sus le leu, et estrain de bendelz.	2. If the thread does not open at the beginning of the fringe, then lightly open it when it appears; then pull it as we have said, and then smooth out the drapery with your hands and put it on the shoulder, and hold it tightly.
Et si a de tels homes qui broient seil et mettent sus por corrompre cele moistor qui est demoree.	3. And if such men who bribe seal and put on to corrupt the moisture which is dried out.
Puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then the cure, as long as he is healthy.
